<BR>
<BR>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:13pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<TABLE style="margin-right:111.6pt; font-size:10pt" cellspacing=0><TR><TD valign=top><P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><img src="pressrelease991001.jpg" alt="[pressrelease991001.jpg]" align=middle height=67.733 width=192.067>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
</TD><TD valign=top><P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Arial; font-size:22pt; color:#00007F" align=right><U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NEWS</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; line-height:9.5pt; font-family:Tahoma; font-size:7.5pt; color:#3F3F3F" align=right>FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</P>
</TD></TR>
</TABLE>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:13pt" align=center><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; line-height:15pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:13pt" align=center><B>CROSS COUNTRY HEALTHCARE TO PRESENT AT </B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; line-height:15pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:13pt" align=center><B>JPMORGAN HEALTHCARE CONFERENCE</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>BOCA RATON, Fla. &#150; December 22, 2004 &#150;</B> Cross Country Healthcare, Inc. (Nasdaq: CCRN) announced today that it is scheduled to make a presentation on Tuesday, January 11, 2005, at 2:30 p.m. Pacific Time at the JPMorgan 23<SUP>rd</SUP> Annual Healthcare Conference being held at the Westin St. Francis Hotel in San Francisco, California.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Cross Country&#146;s presentation will be webcast and accessible to the public online via the Company&#146;s web site at <FONT COLOR=#0000FF><U>www.corporate-ir.net/ireye/ir_site.zhtml?ticker=ccrn&amp;script=2100%20</U></FONT>. &nbsp;Through this link, visitors will be able to access the Company&#146;s presentation made by Joseph A. Boshart, President and Chief Executive Officer of Cross Country Healthcare, Inc., who will provide an overview of Cross Country&#146;s business and prospects. &nbsp;Replays will be available for 90 days after the presentation at the same website address.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Cross Country Healthcare, Inc. is a leading provider of healthcare staffing services in the United States. &nbsp;The Company has a client base of over 3,000 hospitals, pharmaceutical companies and other healthcare providers across all 50 states. &nbsp;Copies of this and other news releases as well as additional information about Cross Country can be obtained online at <FONT COLOR=#0000FF><U>www.crosscountry.com</U></FONT>. &nbsp;Shareholders and prospective investors can also register at the corporate Web site to automatically receive the Company&#146;s press releases by e-mail.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:111.6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:500.4pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><I>The Company&#146;s presentation contains forward-looking statements that are predictive in nature, that depend upon or refer to future events or conditions or that include words such as &#147;expects&#148;, &#147;anticipates&#148;, &#147;intends&#148;, &#147;plans&#148;, &#147;believes&#148;, &#147;estimates&#148; and similar expressions are forward-looking statements. These statements involve known and unknown risks, uncertainties and other factors that may cause our actual results and performance to be materially different from any future results or performance expressed or implied by these forward-looking statements. These factors include our ability to attract and retain qualified nurses and other healthcare personnel, costs and availability of short-term leases for our travel nurses, demand for the healthcare services we provide, both nationally and in the regions in which we o
perate, the functioning of our information systems, the effect of existing or future government regulation and federal and state legislative and enforcement initiatives on our business, our clients&#146; ability to pay us for our services, our ability to successfully implement our acquisition and development strategies, the effect of liabilities and other claims asserted against us, the effect of competition in the markets we serve, and other factors set forth under the caption &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in the Company&#146;s Registration Statement on Form S-3 dated November 3, 2004, or any amendments thereof.</I></P>
